## sap_successfactors_org_create_focost_center

Add new entity to FOCostCenter

**Parameters:**

| Parameter | Type | Required | Default | Description |

## sap_successfactors_org_create_fodivision

Add new entity to FODivision

**Parameters:**

| Parameter | Type | Required | Default | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `businessUnitFlx` | string | No | — | Business Unit Flx |

## sap_successfactors_org_replace_position_matrix_relationship

| Parameter | Type | Required | Default | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `Position_code` | string | Yes | — | key: Position_code |
| `Position_effectiveStartDate` | string | Yes | — | key: Position_effectiveStartDate |
